We say in the introduction of this book that whoever is not knowledgeable about the things mentioned before, if he does not take care, he will fall into error and harm people.
Thus I have seen many of those who engage in this science, and then abandon it, lacking knowledge and experience.
For I see a foolish doctor who treats an abscess on the neck or throat of a woman, and treats the arteries of the neck; because so much blood flowed out that the woman fell dead in his hands.
And I saw another doctor who treated a stone of a man's kidney, and the stone was large; he took out with him a piece of the bladder, and the man died within three days.
And I had already been called by the patient to treat him, and I saw the condition of the patient and the size of the stone, and knew well that if one touched it, he would die.
And I saw another doctor who took in care Duke Henry of our land who had a broken leg, and with the breakage he had a wounded place;
